  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_09dd5653-1849-43ae-b699-ed2477d0f7c4'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();

    <a title="Peter" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/63168028-peter"><img alt="Peter" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1516912354p2/63168028.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2310270553?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Peter" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Peter" href="/user/show/63168028-peter">Peter</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2310270553" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12251527692826749570"><b>Threat</b><br/>This is the third book in the Chronicles of Ancient Darkness series and the story continues with Torak and Renn on a mission to rescue Wolf who has been taken captive by Soul Eaters. The soul eaters are a demonic evil power that exists and seems to be targeting him. The rescue is no doubt a trap but Torak must try and save his pack brother. <br/><br/>The excitement continues at the pace of the first 2 books, and there is now a growing attraction to Torak, Wolf and Renn as their characters develop. T</span>
  <span id="freeText12251527692826749570" style="display:none"><b>Threat</b><br />This is the third book in the Chronicles of Ancient Darkness series and the story continues with Torak and Renn on a mission to rescue Wolf who has been taken captive by Soul Eaters. The soul eaters are a demonic evil power that exists and seems to be targeting him. The rescue is no doubt a trap but Torak must try and save his pack brother. <br /><br />The excitement continues at the pace of the first 2 books, and there is now a growing attraction to Torak, Wolf and Renn as their characters develop. Torak is still only a child so he needs reminding from adults on how to behave and recognise authority.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/587002077?book_show_action=true">Apr 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chanelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chanelle" href="/user/show/7860660-chanelle">Chanelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780060728335" href="/book/show/1186709.Soul_Eater">review of another edition</a>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7860660-chanelle?shelf=apt-titles">apt-titles</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7860660-chanelle?shelf=fave-character-s">fave-character-s</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7860660-chanelle?shelf=thriller">thriller</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7860660-chanelle?shelf=junior-ya">junior-ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7860660-chanelle?shelf=witches">witches</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer587002077" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8294437740671599699">I read this one so quickly that I didn’t even have time to put it on my currently reading list before I began <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/870821.Outcast__Chronicles_of_Ancient_Darkness___4_' title='Outcast (Chronicles of Ancient Darkness, #4) by Michelle Paver' rel='nofollow noopener'>Outcast</a>. <br/><br/>The first thing I have to say is Michelle Paver (so far) seems to be naming her books very precisely. It’s simple yet very apt plus it mimics the subtle intensity of the action and the prose in this book. Another very subtle event is the developing relationship between Torak and Renn as they try to navigate their growing friendship. <br/><br/>Renn’s characterization is so cool. She's beco</span>
  <span id="freeText8294437740671599699" style="display:none">I read this one so quickly that I didn’t even have time to put it on my currently reading list before I began <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/870821.Outcast__Chronicles_of_Ancient_Darkness___4_" title="Outcast (Chronicles of Ancient Darkness, #4) by Michelle Paver" rel="nofollow noopener">Outcast</a>. <br /><br />The first thing I have to say is Michelle Paver (so far) seems to be naming her books very precisely. It’s simple yet very apt plus it mimics the subtle intensity of the action and the prose in this book. Another very subtle event is the developing relationship between Torak and Renn as they try to navigate their growing friendship. <br /><br />Renn’s characterization is so cool. She's becoming one of my favourite literary heroines. She proves her courage and wisdom yet again. And it’s also bolstered by how Torak perceives her strength, intelligence, integrity and bravery. <br /><br />She's also a great balance to Torak's seemingly grimmer nature. So far, especially with each new puzzle he uncovers about his past, Torak becomes less carefree and relaxed with the new family he creates with the Ravens. <br /> <br />In fact this book has been the darkest one so far! It becomes more apparently good versus evil here. I am reminded of reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5.Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban__Harry_Potter___3_" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (Harry Potter, #3) by J.K. Rowling" rel="nofollow noopener">Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban</a>. That, to me at least, was the book which really changed it from a simple school story to a very dangerous adventure. <br /><br />Things are definitely getting more serious as this book ends and the title of the fourth has an ominous ring, but I am perversely excited to see what else will happen to Torak. </span>
  <a data-text-id="8294437740671599699" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText13537476905555149714" style="display:none">"Soul Eater" is the third book in "Chronicles of Ancient Darkness", but there will be six books in all.<br /><br />The story continues to follow Renn and Torak in their pursuit of the Soul Eaters, who have captured wolf; Torak's canine companion and ‘pack brother’. Wolf is to be used in a series of sacrifices to protect the Soul Eaters from the demons they are to unleash into the world.<br /><br />Torak and Renn pursue the Soul Eaters and try to prevent the evil they wish to release. Torak is a spirit walker and is able to free his souls from his body and enter other creature's bodies. He enters an ice bear’s body multiple times to fight the Soul Eaters, and once he almost loses his souls, but wolf reminds him of his humanity.<br /><br />The book ends in a satisfying way, but I find the story occasionally summarizes events rather than giving us all the fascinating details that would make the story more realistic, compelling and exciting.<br /></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2774457379?book_show_action=true">Apr 07, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennie Louwes" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennie Louwes" href="/user/show/89985522-jennie-louwes">Jennie Louwes</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780060728311" href="/book/show/295321.Soul_Eater">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2774457379" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12178880655365186707">Motherhood affords you an opportunity to discover books you might otherwise gloss over and never pick-up. Passing judgement far too quickly thinking a YA book series is meant for kids. <br/><br/>A YA book series just meant for kids? Not so in regards to the Chronicles of Ancient Darkness! It's a hold on tight, fly by the seat of your pants, non-stop thrill ride! <br/><br/>This 3rd installment, within the series, rivals the first. It's well deserving of a 5 star rating. Why these books haven't been met with the same</span>
  <span id="freeText12178880655365186707" style="display:none">Motherhood affords you an opportunity to discover books you might otherwise gloss over and never pick-up. Passing judgement far too quickly thinking a YA book series is meant for kids. <br /><br />A YA book series just meant for kids? Not so in regards to the Chronicles of Ancient Darkness! It's a hold on tight, fly by the seat of your pants, non-stop thrill ride! <br /><br />This 3rd installment, within the series, rivals the first. It's well deserving of a 5 star rating. Why these books haven't been met with the same acclaim as say the "Harry Potter" books is beyond me. Yes, they're that good (if not better!)<br /><br />"Soul Eater" delves into spiritual warfare and does so deftly. Demons are described as beings that cause "havoc and despair"; "sucking out courage and trust, leaving the seeds of malice and strife" (page 10). Demons cause arguments and dissension between friends as well as doubts in ones own natural abilities and instincts (page 266). They're set upon destruction. <br /><br />Michelle Paver has created an outstanding series. Filled with rich detail. She immerses you in story. You can't help but be drawn in. Bravo to the authoress! <br /><br />Onward, my kids and I go; "Outcast" is up next.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12178880655365186707" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_532782677" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/532782677" />
    <a title="Maythavee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12969590-maythavee"><img alt="Maythavee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1513161414p2/12969590.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/532782677?book_show_action=true">Feb 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maythavee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maythavee" href="/user/show/12969590-maythavee">Maythavee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12969590-maythavee?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer532782677" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9539731163577329629">I knew Michelle Paver wouldn’t let me down. Soul Eater was a fantastic book! My favourite book in the series so far! <br/><br/>I love the characters even more as the series goes on. Paver knew what she was doing and she does it well. I seriously feel bad for Torak. Bad things just keep happening to him. Why can’t he be at peace just for a little longer? Wolf being kidnapped is one of the worst things that could have happened to him. I love his dedication to find Wolf but it also blinded him which caused h</span>
  <span id="freeText9539731163577329629" style="display:none">I knew Michelle Paver wouldn’t let me down. Soul Eater was a fantastic book! My favourite book in the series so far! <br /><br />I love the characters even more as the series goes on. Paver knew what she was doing and she does it well. I seriously feel bad for Torak. Bad things just keep happening to him. Why can’t he be at peace just for a little longer? Wolf being kidnapped is one of the worst things that could have happened to him. I love his dedication to find Wolf but it also blinded him which caused him to do stupid things (like fighting with Renn). Speaking of Renn, she is quickly climbing up the ranks of my favourite female characters. I love her so much! She is just awesome. Torak would not have made it without her. Without Wolf, the interactions between the two were simply great. I love how they knew each other so well but I was also annoyed but them keeping secrets from each other. I just want them to be happy with Wolf okay? (I was so happy when Wolf referred to Renn as his and Torak’s pack sister)<br /><br />The plot was just intense. I was scared for Wolf, Renn and Torak the whole time. We got to meet the rest of the Soul-Eaters and they were so creepy. We also got to see Torak spirit walk several times and it was amazing. Everything about this book was amazing. I loved the backstory about Michelle Paver’s researching trips at the end of the book. They’re so entertaining. Can’t wait to start Outcast!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9539731163577329629" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/351288299" />
    <a title="Candy Wood" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5858970-candy-wood"><img alt="Candy Wood" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1311421258p2/5858970.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/351288299?book_show_action=true">Jun 19, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candy Wood" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candy Wood" href="/user/show/5858970-candy-wood">Candy Wood</a>
      </span>

          added it


          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781842551721" href="/book/show/295328.Soul_Eater">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5858970-candy-wood?shelf=children-s-ya">children-s-ya</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer351288299" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6784785349606601540">Michelle Paver’s Chronicles of Ancient Darkness series so far is a model for how a series ought to work. Like the first two books, this one has a plot that is complete in itself while still building on the earlier books and setting up problems for the next ones. Right away, Wolf is captured by people who turn out to be Soul Eaters, as Torak’s father was before he realized their evil intent, so Torak and Renn set out to find and rescue him. The journey leads them to the Far North, where many chal</span>
  <span id="freeText6784785349606601540" style="display:none">Michelle Paver’s Chronicles of Ancient Darkness series so far is a model for how a series ought to work. Like the first two books, this one has a plot that is complete in itself while still building on the earlier books and setting up problems for the next ones. Right away, Wolf is captured by people who turn out to be Soul Eaters, as Torak’s father was before he realized their evil intent, so Torak and Renn set out to find and rescue him. The journey leads them to the Far North, where many challenges to their survival come from their own unfamiliarity with the terrain as well as from nature and from the Soul Eaters. It’s also impressive that even though Torak and Renn have amazing survival skills and are confronting cosmic evil, they are still children, still learning. And Paver’s research provides learning for readers as well. Recommended.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6784785349606601540" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText10120988402748120864" style="display:none">"We keep our dead with us till spring, said Akoomik, to save them from the foxes. And to stop them feeling left out, Tanugeak added comfortably. They like chatting just as much as we do. When you see a star travelling very fast, that's one of them setting off to visit their friends."<br /><br />Fantastic! Torak and Renn set off on yet another journey only this time they take on the frigid temperatures and ice along with the feared soul eaters. These stories are loads of fun and full of life lessons, true friendships and awesome adventures. I highly recommend these books to anyone who loves a great story and a "goodread". <div id="review_2636050381" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2636050381" />
    <a title="Thomas" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/63824806-thomas"><img alt="Thomas" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484326813p2/63824806.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2636050381?book_show_action=true">Mar 31, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Thomas" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Thomas" href="/user/show/63824806-thomas">Thomas</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer2636050381&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2636050381" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5174579219013745500">Soul Eater returned to the spectacular standard of Wolf Brother, both in terms of how much I enjoyed it and regarding the quality of the writing. Paver took the reader to some very dark places and I am quite surprised this can be categized as a children’s book.<br/><br/>The previous summer Torak, Renn and Wolf managed to defeat the Soul Eater Tenris the Seal Mage and in doing so, saved the lands from the sickness he had created. Now the grip of winter is upon Torak’s world and Wolf has been taken by the o</span>
  <span id="freeText5174579219013745500" style="display:none">Soul Eater returned to the spectacular standard of Wolf Brother, both in terms of how much I enjoyed it and regarding the quality of the writing. Paver took the reader to some very dark places and I am quite surprised this can be categized as a children’s book.<br /><br />The previous summer Torak, Renn and Wolf managed to defeat the Soul Eater Tenris the Seal Mage and in doing so, saved the lands from the sickness he had created. Now the grip of winter is upon Torak’s world and Wolf has been taken by the other mysterious Soul Eaters. Torak and Renn must now brave the remote Far North in order to rescue him.<br /><br />As with the previous two books, Paver, in my opinion, makes her world feel so real by the quality of the research she has performed. It is clear she has experienced the harsh nature of the polar environment and come face to face with its creatures, particularly the polar bears and is able to express her experience so well such that I was vividly able to imagine every step of the story.<br /><br />As suggested from the title of the book, the Soul Eaters certainly made a lasting impression when we at last met them, particularly Thiazzi, who I had an intense dislike for since I first read the series, and I considered him a sadistic bully.<br /><br />Soul Eater fully deserves 5 stars, perhaps in some ways it was even better than Wolf Brother. Onto the second half of the series with Torak’s next adventure Outcast.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5174579219013745500" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_753451722" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/753451722" />
    <a title="Anna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4552039-anna"><img alt="Anna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1579546503p2/4552039.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/753451722?book_show_action=true">Oct 31, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anna" href="/user/show/4552039-anna">Anna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781842551721" href="/book/show/295328.Soul_Eater">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4552039-anna?shelf=prehistorical-fiction">prehistorical-fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer753451722" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3434107346793178220">'Soul Eater' takes us to the Far North as Torak and Renn venture to save Wolf. They go where not many people dare to enter, and therefore our heroes are alone for most of the book. However, it didn't tire me out. This also means that there's only Torak, Renn and Wolf to stand against Soul Eaters and a whole horde of demons. Their outstanding courage really astounded me. We got to see Torak spirit walk deliberately, and the process is not as harmless and pleasant as I thought it to be. And the fa</span>
  <span id="freeText3434107346793178220" style="display:none">'Soul Eater' takes us to the Far North as Torak and Renn venture to save Wolf. They go where not many people dare to enter, and therefore our heroes are alone for most of the book. However, it didn't tire me out. This also means that there's only Torak, Renn and Wolf to stand against Soul Eaters and a whole horde of demons. Their outstanding courage really astounded me. We got to see Torak spirit walk deliberately, and the process is not as harmless and pleasant as I thought it to be. And the fact Torak invokes it on purpose makes it even more amazing. Another thing that impressed me is the depth of bonds between Torak and Wolf. It goes so far that Torak allows Wolf to bite him, knowing he can lose a hand if the latter panics, and Wolf allows Torak to hurt him knowing Torak only wants to help him. <br /><br />Again, Michelle Paver created fantastic atmosphere in her book. I like the descriptions of the Far North and the amount of details of Ice Clans' life. And every time an ice bear appeared I could sense that air of magnificence, strength and wilderness. Excellent job, Michelle!<br /><br />Unlike in previous books, Soul Eaters don't hide their true faces, and they are hideous. Oak Mage is a sadistic brute; Bat Mage is willing to sacrifice lives for her goal; Viper Mage is like an apple filled with worms - beautiful outside, but rotten inside; and Eagle Owl Mage is practically all dead inside. Besides, we learn a lot about Soul Eaters. What are their goals? How are they able to control demons? What really happened during the Great Fire that almost destroyed Soul Eaters? Eye of Viper cave is just as creepy - normally I like underground actions, but Michelle Paver creates such an eerie air and conveys the feeling of damp, stuffy and cramped place. The rituals held to find the Door and to summon demons were terrifying so I could almost feel demons' presence.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3434107346793178220" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1447910012" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1447910012" />
    <a title="Big Pete" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/47746222-big-pete"><img alt="Big Pete" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1469016966p2/47746222.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1447910012?book_show_action=true">Nov 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Big Pete" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Big Pete" href="/user/show/47746222-big-pete">Big Pete</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1447910012" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18074195816765342852"><i>Soul Eater</i> opens in the silence of the forest as winter sets in. Torak and Renn are hunting, and Torak notices an owl feather lying upon the snow. He hopes it's not a bad omen. It is. <br/>In moments, Wolf is abducted and Torak and Renn hunt his pursuers, venturing into the far north, where nothing is as it seems and one slip upon the ice can spell your doom...<br/><i>Soul Eater</i> is a much darker book than <i>Wolf Brother</i> and <i>Spirit Walker</i>, with less action and more travelling, but when violence comes it is sava</span>
  <span id="freeText18074195816765342852" style="display:none"><i>Soul Eater</i> opens in the silence of the forest as winter sets in. Torak and Renn are hunting, and Torak notices an owl feather lying upon the snow. He hopes it's not a bad omen. It is. <br />In moments, Wolf is abducted and Torak and Renn hunt his pursuers, venturing into the far north, where nothing is as it seems and one slip upon the ice can spell your doom...<br /><i>Soul Eater</i> is a much darker book than <i>Wolf Brother</i> and <i>Spirit Walker</i>, with less action and more travelling, but when violence comes it is savage and brutal. The relationships between the characters are more widely explored, as Torak and Renn's friendship is tested to the breaking point on their journey. <br />The Soul Eaters make a collective appearance, all of the survivors coming together for a twisted ritual that warps the code of the Forest clans. We get more than a glimpse of this shadowy cabal, learning the names and faces of its members. Thiazzi the Oak Mage is a sadistic giant, as strong and unyielding as his Clan's symbol. Seshru the Viper Mage is a rotten heart hidden beneath a beautiful exterior. Nef the Bat Mage is a melancholic, sympathetic character who nonetheless is willing to kill for her goals. And then there is Eostra, the enigmatic Eagle Owl Mage, the spectral mastermind behind the cabal's plans. <br />We get a fascinating look at the lifestyle of the Ice Clans, how they hunt and survive in their frozen homeland. <i>Soul Eater</i> is the novel where Paver's prose really hits the peak, reaching an area where it is perfect to read for all ages. She creates a claustrophobic cavern where the foul rituals take place, constructing a frozen tundra where you can feel the icy wind bite into you. <br />I really enjoyed re-reading <i>Soul Eater</i> and I have no reservations about recommending it. </span>
  <a data-text-id="18074195816765342852" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5221314253845872298">Whilst out hunting with Renn, somebody snatches Wolf, and takes him to the Far North. Torak cannot abandon his pack brother, so they follow through unknown territory, but can they make it in time to save Wolf?<br/><br/>Again, another fantastic addition to the series. I'm really enjoying these books, you can tell the amount of research the author has done because it's so realistically detailed for that time. The stories have started to get darker in tone as Torak and Renn get closer to fighting the Soul Ea</span>
  <span id="freeText5221314253845872298" style="display:none">Whilst out hunting with Renn, somebody snatches Wolf, and takes him to the Far North. Torak cannot abandon his pack brother, so they follow through unknown territory, but can they make it in time to save Wolf?<br /><br />Again, another fantastic addition to the series. I'm really enjoying these books, you can tell the amount of research the author has done because it's so realistically detailed for that time. The stories have started to get darker in tone as Torak and Renn get closer to fighting the Soul Eaters, and with the end of every book, you never know where the next one will go, so it's always unexpected and interesting. A really enjoyable series so far, and I'm already thinking ahead and wondering what will happen in the last book, so I cannot wait to read the next three and find out! </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2844611693?book_show_action=true">Aug 27, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Travis Berketa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Travis Berketa" href="/user/show/8307433-travis-berketa">Travis Berketa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781842551721" href="/book/show/295328.Soul_Eater">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2844611693" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12653633699760250357">So, I'm still in two minds about the <b>
  <i>Chronicles of Ancient Darkness</i>
</b> series; I want to see how the story of Torak unravels, but I find Torak and Renn (the main characters) annoying. There's the Catch 22 - I need to read about these characters that I don't really like in order to find out about the story.<br/><br/>Anyway, this third book of the series, <b>
  <i>Soul Eater</i>
</b>, tells us about the lone Wolf Clan boy called Torak having his pack-brother, Wolf (a real wolf), taken by a group of evil sorcerers called</span>
  <span id="freeText12653633699760250357" style="display:none">So, I'm still in two minds about the <b>
  <i>Chronicles of Ancient Darkness</i>
</b> series; I want to see how the story of Torak unravels, but I find Torak and Renn (the main characters) annoying. There's the Catch 22 - I need to read about these characters that I don't really like in order to find out about the story.<br /><br />Anyway, this third book of the series, <b>
  <i>Soul Eater</i>
</b>, tells us about the lone Wolf Clan boy called Torak having his pack-brother, Wolf (a real wolf), taken by a group of evil sorcerers called Soul Eaters. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The Soul Eaters plan to kill Wolf and other hunters (which is against Clan Law) in order to release the demons from the Otherworld and control them for their own means. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Torak sets out on his own to find Wolf, which makes Renn upset, because she was not told and therefore feels that the boy does not trust her... And that's where the frustration begins to mount!<br /><br />It was extremely annoying to continue reading how Torak and Renn were close - Torak sees Renn as one of the only people he can depend upon, besides Wolf, and it appears that Renn has feelings for Torak - BUT - they continually keep things secret from one another... and not anything life changing - stupid secrets! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I do not understand - even though the book states that Torak fears Renn will want to run away - why Torak would keep the secret of Wolf being taken by the Soul Eaters. I do not understand why Renn would keep the secret of Wolf being taken by the Soul Eaters (Yes, they're both keeping the same secret!). It's even more annoying when they share their secret and then decide to keep more secrets from one another, even though they've just had a whole moment of "we've been keeping secrets from each other, maybe we should be honest". <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> And this goes on right to the end of the book, where Torak keeps another secret from Renn.<br /><br />I would much rather the author, Michelle Paver, make up her mind about where these two characters stand with each other and write it that way, because they both come across as mopey and forever "fearing that they'll be found out".<br /><br />I like the story that is being told, but not the way it is unfolding.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12653633699760250357" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780060728311" href="/book/show/295321.Soul_Eater">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Anyone looking for a fun adventure story!!!!!</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/56506626-brittney-tyler?shelf=personal-library">personal-library</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2085810063" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9342272281744766507">Star Rating: 4 stars<br/><br/>Note: This is the 3rd book in the Chronicles of Ancient Darkness so this will not be an in-depth review. <br/><br/>Needing a break from all the complex, library books I was reading, I decided to pick up Soul Eater by Michelle Paver, the 3rd book in the Chronicles of Ancient Darkness series to continue my re-read of the series. This series tells the story of Torak, a young Wolf Clan boy, from 6,000 years ago as he tries to save his world from the dangers of the Soul Eaters. The Soul Eat</span>
  <span id="freeText9342272281744766507" style="display:none">Star Rating: 4 stars<br /><br />Note: This is the 3rd book in the Chronicles of Ancient Darkness so this will not be an in-depth review. <br /><br />Needing a break from all the complex, library books I was reading, I decided to pick up Soul Eater by Michelle Paver, the 3rd book in the Chronicles of Ancient Darkness series to continue my re-read of the series. This series tells the story of Torak, a young Wolf Clan boy, from 6,000 years ago as he tries to save his world from the dangers of the Soul Eaters. The Soul Eaters are clan-mages that have become disillusioned with the World Spirit and have decided to break away for its control so that they can control their own destiny. However, their meddling has drastically affected the safety of the world and everyone in it. <br /><br />My absolute favorite thing about these books is that in each book so far, we have got to explore and learn about a different area of this prehistoric world. For instance, book one showed how clans lived in the Open Forest, while book 2 shows how the Sea Clans live, and this book, book 3, shows how clans in the Far North live. As a lover of history and archaeology, I really loved learning how the different clans survived in these different environments, and I hope that the rest of the series continues to give me this chance.<br /><br />The only thing that I am a little confused about when it comes to this series is I don’t really understand what the conflict is exactly. It has never been explained clearly and I really wished it would be because I am a little confused about what the Soul Eaters are doing and why they need to be stopped. I understand that they are bad, but as to exactly what they are doing and why, I don’t understand. I hope that this gets to be explained in later books.<br /><br />All in all, this is an amazing addition to the series and I can’t wait to keep reading. 4 stars overall!!!!!!<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9342272281744766507" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer2069811333&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2069811333" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12263872335363467309">This was amazing!!<br/><br/>The second book in the series was sort of a downer for me. It wasn't too interesting, so I was a bit scared going into this book. Scared of loosing interest completely. But it just kept getting better and better! The story is very fluent and everything happens so quickly, but not too quickly - You still keep up all the way through.<br/><br/>By the time they had entered the grotto, I was struck with enormous feelings towards these character and actually felt a genuine interest in how they</span>
  <span id="freeText12263872335363467309" style="display:none">This was amazing!!<br /><br />The second book in the series was sort of a downer for me. It wasn't too interesting, so I was a bit scared going into this book. Scared of loosing interest completely. But it just kept getting better and better! The story is very fluent and everything happens so quickly, but not too quickly - You still keep up all the way through.<br /><br />By the time they had entered the grotto, I was struck with enormous feelings towards these character and actually felt a genuine interest in how they were going to make it. All the time there was something new and excising happening! When Renn got stuck and felt claustrophobic, I felt really uneasy too since I really, REALLY hate small spaces. There were also a couple of places where I almost started crying, and felt genuine sad. In the end where it turns out that Torak got marks as a Soul Eater; man, that was amazing! I legit let out a silent gasp as I was listening to it.<br /><br />Michelle's way of describing feelings and the surrounding environment is fantastic. I could feel the cold snow, the harsh ice, the sharp and steamy walls of the grotto. I could taste the seal lard and feel the pain as they went up into the north. She's also an expert at describing the life in the stone age, I feel like I'm learning so much from reading these.<br /><br />This feels like THE book where everything finally happens, like the first two were a buildup to this one, and I'll definitely check out the next book. I must know what happens next!</span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5034163600157153415">Once again, I will say what I have said about this Chronicles of Ancient Darkness Series. It is not a book for children of elementary school age. I would even question it for children of junior high school age. Once a teen or adult though, one would have to know the person. For myself personally, I found some parts upsetting and difficult to read. There are portions of the book which are about animal cruelty which were very upsetting to me. Also, there were portions about demons and sacrifice wh</span>
  <span id="freeText5034163600157153415" style="display:none">Once again, I will say what I have said about this Chronicles of Ancient Darkness Series. It is not a book for children of elementary school age. I would even question it for children of junior high school age. Once a teen or adult though, one would have to know the person. For myself personally, I found some parts upsetting and difficult to read. There are portions of the book which are about animal cruelty which were very upsetting to me. Also, there were portions about demons and sacrifice which were hard for me to read. <br /><br />On the positive side, it is a very exciting book and very fast paced. The author's extensive research on old tribes of people and their customs really made the book interesting. Also, her research on animals and their habits shone through on the pages of this book. Sometimes, I felt that I could see through the eyes of these animals and it was a wonderful, exhilarating feeling. <br /><br />In conclusion, I would say the good parts of this book were worth the bad once you look at it as a whole story. It all fits together.</span>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

              <span id="reviewTextContainer3079842594" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer2372895579921420871">The previous two books were good, but something really clicked with this one! It's like all the characters and the setting are really meshing together all of a sudden. This one is also a lot darker than the books before, and a lot of very serious plot points happened which I thought would have been saved for the final book, so I was surprised! I also really enjoyed meeting the White Fox Clan. The villains and their actions/goal were really quite scary at times and I think they caused a few night</span>
  <span id="freeText2372895579921420871" style="display:none">The previous two books were good, but something really clicked with this one! It's like all the characters and the setting are really meshing together all of a sudden. This one is also a lot darker than the books before, and a lot of very serious plot points happened which I thought would have been saved for the final book, so I was surprised! I also really enjoyed meeting the White Fox Clan. The villains and their actions/goal were really quite scary at times and I think they caused a few nightmares for me.</span>

<div id="review_2296213367" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2296213367" />
    <a title="Johnny Bennett" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/554177-johnny-bennett"><img alt="Johnny Bennett" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/m_50x66-82093808bca726cb3249a493fbd3bd0f.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2296213367?book_show_action=true">Feb 14, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Johnny Bennett" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Johnny Bennett" href="/user/show/554177-johnny-bennett">Johnny Bennett</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780060728335" href="/book/show/1186709.Soul_Eater">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2296213367" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11388336078625746836">Soul Eater is a darker tale and more transitional, clearly feeling like it is a setup book for something bigger. The pacing seems okay but does seem adventure along in spurts instead of driving to the end. There continues to be a view of demons in this book that some might be uncomfortable with and it becomes only stronger as you progress. On the other hand, the title is Soul Eater, so one might expect something like that.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer11893995857178908529">Another fantastic book in the series. <br/><br/>The only thing that bothered me slightly is that the adventure practically starts on the first page. There is no 'wading into it' with a tiny summary of what has happened since the last book's ending, or some other kind of explanation. Just directly the suspense that comes with adventures. <br/>Despite this, it was a such a delight to once again delve into the story that has enriched my childhood. <br/><br/>Torak has a wolf grin. And Renn has a sharp-toothed smile. <br/>What I </span>
  <span id="freeText11893995857178908529" style="display:none">Another fantastic book in the series. <br /><br />The only thing that bothered me slightly is that the adventure practically starts on the first page. There is no 'wading into it' with a tiny summary of what has happened since the last book's ending, or some other kind of explanation. Just directly the suspense that comes with adventures. <br />Despite this, it was a such a delight to once again delve into the story that has enriched my childhood. <br /><br />Torak has a wolf grin. And Renn has a sharp-toothed smile. <br />What I love about these descriptions is that they are so unique and scarcely shared during their adventures. Adventures which I will always love to re-read.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('LUMHZe25UgosDSOhh+PA46hTjO0wlNRDmRe5sWcUFkBF8Wh3Kfo1iNYDjtPpcP53DGJDzGMtc3XSx43o0P7jPQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('6Z7MOsRW9fVWBW25NWeQX7jhpB4id/C7utjCPfSokZSBLKMoABWSd6wLwMtb9K7LHNBrP3HOV43xCPZkQ0Jk6Q==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer8336832947550071135">Michelle Paver was born in Central Africa, but came to England as a child. After gaining a degree in Biochemistry from Oxford University, she became a partner in a City law firm, but eventually gave that up to write full-time.<br/><br/>The hugely successful <i>Chronicles of Ancient Darkness</i> series arose from Michelle's lifelong passion for animals, anthropology and the distant past - as as well as an encounter</span>
  <span id="freeText8336832947550071135" style="display:none">Michelle Paver was born in Central Africa, but came to England as a child. After gaining a degree in Biochemistry from Oxford University, she became a partner in a City law firm, but eventually gave that up to write full-time.<br /><br />The hugely successful <i>Chronicles of Ancient Darkness</i> series arose from Michelle's lifelong passion for animals, anthropology and the distant past - as as well as an encounter with a large bear in a remote valley in southern California. To research the books, Michelle has traveled to Finland, Greenland, Sweden, Norway, Arctic Canada and the Carpathian Mountains. She has slept on reindeer skins, swum with wild orca (killer whales), and got nose-to-nose with polar bears - and, of course, wolves. </span>
  <a data-text-id="8336832947550071135" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

For two summers Torak and Renn have been living in the Forest with their faithful pack-brother, Wolf. But their happiness is shattered when Renn realizes Torak is in danger – and she\'s the threat. When she mysteriously disappears, Torak and Wolf brave the Far North to find her. At the mercy of the Sea Mother and haunted by ravenous ice bears, their quest leads them to the Edge of the World. There they must face an enemy more evil than any they\'ve encountered. Viper\'s Daughter plunges you back into the Stone-Age world of Torak, Renn and Wolf: a world of demons, Hidden People and exhilarating adventure which has entranced millions of readers. PRAISE FOR VIPER\'S DAUGHTER: \'What rich, dazzling, immersive storytelling ... The best book I have read this year by a country mile. (By a wild arctic length of many wolf lopes, I suppose I should say)\' Hilary McKay, author of The Skylarks\' War. \'Michelle is in a league of her own with this series and what luck for us all that she hasn\'t finished with Torak, Renn and Wolf\'s world yet\' Abi Elphinstone, author of Rumblestar. \'Viper\'s Daughter is sharp, striking, and loaded with the wisdom of the deep past. I am in awe of Paver\'s accomplishment\' Sophie Anderson, author of The House with Chicken Legs. \'Skillful, satisfying, and minutely researched, this powerful evocation of an ancient world is vivid in its imagery and captivating in its excitement\' Adrienne Byrne, Muswell Hill Children\'s Bookshop. \'Paver\'s love for the natural world comes across so strongly in her writing and her imagination takes you on a twisting, fantastic journey all the way to the Edge of the World\' Grace Barrett, Waterstones Norwich. <\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"14194713225716850056\" href=\"#\"
